<Review>I've ordered 2 times from this location through the app. The first time it took me 70 minutes to get my pizza, but the App gave me a free medium so I was fine with it. This time I ordered 2 mediums. 1 Buffalo ranch and 1 chicken Alfredo. The App said I would get my order from 20 - 45 minutes. I live 1 mile away so I thought it would be quick. I end up getting my order 90 minutes later and get 2 chicken alfredos. 1 box even had the right label for a Buffalo ranch so I'm not sure how they messed that up. I called afterwards and had someone try to get me off the phone quickly and just tell me I would get store credit for the pizza they got wrong, so there's that atleast.
Edit: picked up my medium store credit. I ordered a Chicken Buffalo ranch pizza. They skimped on the Chicken and Buffalo sauce, so it was more of a ranch pizza than anything. Still haven't heard back from corporate so I'm just done with Dominoes.< /Review>< pics>

<Review>The reason I like Empire mowers, it's because I respect and support small business owners. <Resp>None</Resp><username>Mike Anderson</username>< review>
I'm done with Panda Express. 1. For almost $9, I expect a human sized portion, not a kids menu plate. Give me a break. 2. I've come to the conclusion that if you don't go inside, but through the drive thru, your portion will be a kid size portion. 3. Eaten a few times in the past at this specific location, and have told my family that the chow mein is dry, as is the fried rice. Against my better judgement, I agreed to another visit. My kid drove through the drive thru, brought the food home. Yup, just like before the chow mein and the fried rice were dry, and the portions ridiculously small. Poor reviews on your own site, and Google say to go in, and not through the drive thru if you want to not get ripped off. The drive thru portion is just small, and terrible. I'm finished/done with Panda Express. By the way, the chicken was very good. Will my little ($27.00 total) family order make a difference to them? Probably not. I shouldn't have to wait till I get home to discover poor service. There are many authentic Chinese food joints that don't charge $9 (or close to it) for a real adult portioned meal. Don't expect any good recommendations from me, but I will definitely recommend not patronizing this place.<//review>

< Review>
Want to have your tooth removed? This is your place. I came to this office for my last 2 wisdom teeth removal, after being transferred from 2 other dental offices. The bottom one was a very large tooth and impacted the one next to it. Doctor Yao was very patient and gentle on my case. She made sure that the area was completely numb/painless before she started on the procedure. It seriously took her only 15 MINUTES to get the top wisdom tooth out. NO KIDDING. My teeth are hard and sturdy as rock. Before my braces, an average size male doctor tried to pull my pre-molar. It cost him more than 1 HOUR and 2 BREAKS in the middle to get the job done. The bottom one was a bit trickier, but still not a big problem to Dr. Yao. Two other offices transferred me to a specialist because of this tooth, but to Dr. Yao it was just a simple surgical procedure. She had to cut it in half to get it out. Sewed the wound in and let me walk out of the office in the next 45 minutes. The wounds stopped bleeding the day after with a mild fever (which is normal for tooth removal). I can't thank her enough for saving me a trip to specialist just to have the same thing done. Noticed one thing that she's really not a talker. I supposed she's just like me. The park has potential but seems the city hasn't kept it up. Some neat hut like picnic areas, plethora of benches some shaded some not. Restroom building looks like a shady shack.
